commit 4318d8099245b1eae9bfdbdf4efdcd81266a2cff
Author: tcarlson <tcarlson>
Date:   Fri May 13 19:40:30 2011 +0000

    - Re-use <commit-transaction> / <rollback-transaction> elements for BL-511
    - Allow a RollbackMethod to be passed into the exception strategy so that message delivery can be atomic even when transactions are not configured (BL-412)
    - TransactionTemplate can start, join, and commit transactions, but if an exception occurs, leave transaction handling up to the Exception Strategy, otherwise this causes problems with the DLQ pattern (fixes MULE-5554/EE-2243, enables BL-511)
    - Clean up ExceptionStrategy class hierarchy + API (cleanup that ideally should have been done as part of 3.1), rename DefaultServiceExceptionStrategy to DefaultMessagingExceptionStrategy
    - Delete RollbackRoutingExceptionStrategy and RouteableExceptionStrategy as the standard DefaultMessagingExceptionStrategy can be used instead

commit 64620d6800652d1201c65c30ffb6c5e95c827b26
Author: tcarlson <tcarlson>
Date:   Fri Aug 27 02:48:29 2010 +0000

    Blocked revisions 18641 via svnmerge
    
    ........
      r18641 | epere4 | 2010-07-29 18:09:50 -0300 (Thu, 29 Jul 2010) | 2 lines
    
      MULE-4955 Refactor Exception Strategy invocation so we don't get exception strategies invoked twice
      Changed the strategy for marking an exception as handled. Instead of using an instance variable on the exception (which only work for the exceptions wrapped by some of the ones that we control: instances of MuleException and MuleRuntimeException), we now use a ThreadLocal variable that contains a reference to the exception being handled on the current thread. So if the same thread tries to handle it again, it will be able to avoid doing so.
    ........
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://svn.codehaus.org/mule/branches/mule-3.x@19237 bf997673-6b11-0410-b953-e057580c5b09

      MULE-4927: Exception strategy invoked both for connector *and* service exception strategies when exception on sync outbound endpoint
      Now, when the dispatchToOutboundRouter() method gets an exception from the outbound router and that exception is a DispatchException then we assume that it was handled by the connector-exception-strategy so we ignore it. Otherwise, we rethrow it.
      I had to add a method in ExceptionUtils to detect if the exception was caused by a DispatchException (because it is wrapped by other exceptions, so I cannot simply use instanceof).

commit 5b753b15d3b6d401962c0031c2ba65ff1b16d670
Author: tcarlson <tcarlson>
Date:   Tue Jul 29 19:00:01 2008 +0000

    Merged revisions 12247-12265 via svnmerge from
    https://svn.codehaus.org/mule/branches/mule-2.0.x
    
    ........
      r12247 | dfeist | 2008-07-07 16:25:01 -0500 (Mon, 07 Jul 2008) | 1 line
    
      MULE-3321 Implement Component Notifications, MULE-3524 Message events should not be fired by default
    ........
      r12248 | dandiep | 2008-07-07 17:08:28 -0500 (Mon, 07 Jul 2008) | 15 lines
    
      Support efficient transformations when proxying web services. We
      can now take a StAX message, send it into SAXON as SAX events,
      then write the resulting SAX events directly to the web service
      response.
    
      This magic is done via a new class called DelayedResult. Because
      we don't want to have to write the transformed XML to memory,
      we create a DelayedResult which allows someone down the stream
      to control how the XML is written. In this case, CXF passes in
      a new Result so SAXON can write directly to the XMLStreamWriter.
    
      I had to change DefaultMuleMessage so it recognized other
      consumable types besides InputStream. Feedback on whether or not
      there is a better way to do this is immensely welcome.
    ........

commit 00c2c7a15b5175ebc853de2744ec61eb76ba7633
Author: tcarlson <tcarlson>
Date:   Fri Nov 9 16:46:53 2007 +0000

    Convert test to be XML config-based and update for 2.x.
    The test has changed slightly because it used to programatically create a component, register and unregister it, which would implicitly start/stop the component in 1.x.  The XML-based component now has initialState="stopped", and the test explicitly starts and stops it.  Note that it is impossible to unregister a component from the SpringRegistry since it is read-only!

      - No class casting in lookup methods
    
    - Renamed RegistryFacade to Registry, cleaned up cruft from old Registry incarnation (MULE-2114)
    
    - Removed QuickConfigurationBuilder (MULE-2203).  Everything done with the QuickConfigurationBuilder can be done using the standard registry methods.  Moved a few convenience methods for creating MuleDescriptors into org.mule.tck.MuleTestUtils
    
    - Instead of getting ManagementContext from Registry (which doesn't make any sense to me: MULE-2161), keep singleton ManagementContext in MuleServer (seems like a good place since there should be one ManagementContext per running Mule instance; in a clustered environment the Registry may be shared)
    
    - Since Mule can't really function without a ManagementContext, moved createManagementContext() up from FunctionalTestCase to AbstractMuleTestCase.  Now the ManagementContext is always _created_ by AbstractMuleTestCase, but not started by default.  It _is_ started by default for FunctionalTestCase (related to MULE-1988).
    
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://svn.codehaus.org/mule/branches/mule-2.x@8057 bf997673-6b11-0410-b953-e057580c5b09
